We bring together drivers, businesses, automakers, policymakers, utilities and other stakeholders to make e-mobility a global reality.<\u002Fp> \n <p> Since our founding in 2007, ChargePoint has focused solely on making the transition to electric easy for businesses, fleets and drivers. The Senior Validation Engineer will be analyzing complex designs, defining requirements and test plans, and is able to take ownership of new development projects from start to finish. The ideal candidate is passionate about identifying vulnerabilities and shortcomings of advanced hardware systems, and enjoys working cross-functionally to drive the issues to closure.<\u002Fp>\n <br> reviews<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Analyse parametric and functional test results from manufacturing facilities<\u002Fli> \n  <li>Ensure product integrity and lead design improvements via a data-driven process<\u002Fli> \n <\u002Ful> \n <h3 class=\"jobSectionHeader\"><b>Requirements<\u002Fb><\u002Fh3> \n <ul>\n  <li>Bachelor's Degree in engineering (or advanced degree) with a minimum of 3 years of
